<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><b>SECTION 2 &#8211; <span style="text-transform: uppercase">Financial
Information</span></b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><b>&#160;</b></p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 1in"><b>Item 2.02</b></td><td><b>Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</b></td></tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">We have issued a shareholder letters concerning our revenue results, our
anticipated revenue results for 2022, our plans to list on Nasdaq, potential acquisitions and other matters.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">The shareholder letters are furnished with this Current Report on Form
8-K as Exhibits 99.1-99.4. The information furnished under this Item 2.02 and Item 9.01 of this Current Report on Form 8-K, including
Exhibits 99.1-99.4, shall not be deemed to be &#8220;filed&#8221; for the purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934,
as amended, or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, nor shall it be deemed incorporated by reference in any registration
statement or other filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, regardless of any general incorporation by reference language
in such filing, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in any such filing.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&#160;</p>

<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="font: 13pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><B>IQST &ndash; iQSTEL Connectivity
And Mobility Services Are More Valuable Than Ever</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 13pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">New York, NY, March 03, 2022
(GLOBE NEWSWIRE) -- iQSTEL, Inc. (OTCQX: IQST) today released a special letter to shareholders addressing prevailing world events in conjunction
with the company&rsquo;s unhampered Nasdaq uplisting objective.&nbsp; The shareholder updates from CEO Leandro Iglesias are included in
their entirety below.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Dear Shareholders:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">While the conflict in Ukraine
is dominating headlines, iQSTEL remains on track to achieving its 2022 revenue and Nasdaq uplisting goals and we remain optimistic about
the future.&nbsp; Let me share with you the cause for my optimism.<BR>
<BR>
iQSTEL is in the business of providing connectivity and mobility.&nbsp; Connectivity and mobility are essential to the foundation of individual
freedom.&nbsp; In light of world events, iQSTEL&rsquo;s business is more valuable than ever.<BR>
<BR>
The global immigrant population is underserved by traditional telecommunications carriers.&nbsp; Today&rsquo;s immigrants, more than ever,
need to be in touch with families and loved ones.&nbsp; Again, iQSTEL&rsquo;s voice and SMS services, built with the immigrant population
in mind, are more valuable than ever.<BR>
<BR>
Likewise, international remittances are more critical than ever for the immigrant population, as is the ability to top-up mobile service
balances.&nbsp; Accordingly, iQSTEL&rsquo;s new Global Money One MAXMO fintech ecosystem is an even more timely product.<BR>
<BR>
As world events drive up petroleum costs, the importance of affordable electric transportation is highlighted and iQSTEL&rsquo;s EVOSS
EV Motorcycle rollout out could not be better timed.<BR>
<BR>
Ultimately, the value iQSTEL&rsquo;s connectivity and mobility services are more clear than ever in light of world events.<BR>
<BR>
Recently, I&rsquo;ve had the opportunity to participate in the Mobile World Congress in Barcelona and check in on the latest technological
trends for the near and long-term future.&nbsp; In reaction to my participation, I&rsquo;m ever more confident in iQSTEL&rsquo;s position
in the global market.<BR>
</P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><TD STYLE="width: 33%">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="width: 34%; text-align: center"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo --><!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD><TD STYLE="width: 33%; text-align: right">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><BR>
SMS communications remain a vital component of the global communications market and are expected to remain a vital component for some
time to come.&nbsp; Trends for SMS communications call for an increase in &ldquo;value and intelligence&rdquo; to be integrated into the
service.&nbsp; With more than 50% of iQSTEL&rsquo;s revenue coming from SMS services, I am confident we are on the right path.<BR>
<BR>
Voice services remain important for critical communications and emotional connection.&nbsp; With more than 20 years of experience in voice
communications, iQSTEL is well established to maintain a steady foothold in the voice market.<BR>
<BR>
Fintech solutions are capturing more and more market share in the global financial services market. iQSTEL&rsquo;s MAXMO offering is an
amazing product that I am confident will stand apart from other Fintech solutions. We are accelerating our global launch.<BR>
<BR>
EV connectivity was also featured at the Mobile World Congress.&nbsp; As a telecommunications company entering the EV market, I assure
you, our EV connectivity is among the best of the best.&nbsp; Our first connected EVOSS EV motorcycles are arriving in Miami today where
we will be producing videos featuring our connected EV solution to support the expansion of our distribution network.<BR>
<BR>
Lastly, let me present updates on three key business development fronts:<BR>
<BR>
1) M&amp;A Campaign: &nbsp;We are currently drafting two separate acquisition agreements. Final terms on both have been agreed to and
we anticipate closing both acquisitions soon.&nbsp; We expect the revenue from both acquisitions to augment our organic 2022 Q2 revenues.<BR>
<BR>
2) Nasdaq Uplisting: The next step in our uplisting path is to complete the 2021 audited financial report. In addition to technically
supporting our Nasdaq application, I anticipate the publication of our 10k annual report to validate iQSTEL&rsquo;s, as of yet, unrecognized
value. In so doing, I remain optimistic that iQSTEL&rsquo;s share price will organically rise to meet the Nasdaq listing requirement and
support our uplisting within the first half of 2022.<BR>
</P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><TD STYLE="width: 33%">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="width: 34%; text-align: center"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->2<!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD><TD STYLE="width: 33%; text-align: right">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><BR>
3) $1 Billion Objective: On behalf of all iQSTEL Management and all members of the Independent Board of Directors, I know our Nasdaq uplisiting
is an important milestone. However, I want to keep this milestone in perspective as one small part of iQSTEL&rsquo;s overall objective
of reaching and surpassing a $1 Billion valuation.<BR>
<BR>
Thanks for your support. Please know that management and the Independent Board of<BR>
Directors remain committed to working every single day to achieve our business and<BR>
corporate objectives.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Sincerely,<BR>
<I>Leandro Iglesias</I><BR>
CEO</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">iQSTEL Inc. (OTCQX: IQST)
(<U>www.iQSTEL.com</U>) is a US-based publicly-listed company holding an Independent Board of Directors and Independent Audit Committee
offering leading-edge services through its two business divisions and each of them with independent brands. The B2B division, Brand IQSTelecom
offering Telecommunications, Internet of Things, Technology and Blockchain platforms services, the target market for the B2B division
is Global Markets. The B2C division, Brand EVOSS offering EV Electric Motorcycles, Fintech Ecosystem, the target market for this business
division is Latin America, and the Spanish speakers in the USA. The company has presence in 15 countries, and its products and services
are used in several industries as Telecommunications, Electric Vehicle (EV), Financial Services, Chemical and Liquid Fuel Distribution
Industries. IQSTEL announced on February 17th 2021 that it became a Debt Free Company and is now completely debt free with no Convertible
Notes, Warrants, Promissory Notes or Settlement Agreements from its Balance Sheet.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 13pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><B>IQST &ndash; iQSTEL Initiates
Nasdaq Application Process On Schedule</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 13pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">New York, NY, March 17, 2022
(GLOBE NEWSWIRE) -- iQSTEL, Inc. (OTCQX: IQST) today released an update highlighting the company&rsquo;s latest progress toward its 2022
objectives to include reaching a $90 million revenue forecast and uplisting to Nasdaq in the first half of this year. The shareholder
updates from CEO Leandro Iglesias are included in their entirety below.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Dear Shareholders:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Leading news headlines continue
to impact investor sentiment and weigh on the overall market.&nbsp; There is no need for me to review the news here.&nbsp; We all get
enough of it elsewhere.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">In spite of all the prevailing
headlines, iQSTEL is proceeding in 2022 as planned.&nbsp; We remain on course to achieve our $90 million annual revenue projection and
realize our planned uplisting to Nasdaq within the first half of this year.&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">We are optimistic the global
events currently dominating headlines will be curtailed by the resilience of our global community that has historically endured and overcome
time and time again.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Here at iQSTEL, we will do
our part by maintaining a steady course. We have no doubt that optimism will soon begin to return and be reflected in the overall market.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">As part of our efforts to
remain on course, we continue in the performance testing of our EVOSS electric motorcycles in Miami.&nbsp; Look for an announcement coming
soon on the final results.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">The EVOSS is designed to compete
with the 125 cc combustion engine motorcycle.&nbsp; Our EVOSS comes with three motor options &ndash; 2 Kw, 3 Kw, and 4 Kw.&nbsp; We expect
our performance test results to demonstrate the overall reliability of the EVOSS to include exceptional autonomy supported by our battery
solution, and all at a competitive price.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">In addition to sharing the
performance test results, we plan to soon release a full set of pictures and videos featuring the EVOSS.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">We are enjoying high demand
from dealers for the EVOSS in response to our initial product introductions.&nbsp; We are following up with a digital product brochure
in Spanish and English to soon be delivered to potential dealers via our YouTube Channel. We expect to soon report our first pre-orders
and overall sales projections for Latin America, Europe and Africa.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">With our sights set on
competing as a long-term and comprehensive EV solution provider, our product development department is hard and work on the design of
our next generation of EV products to expand our overall EV market sector reach.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">&nbsp;</P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><TD STYLE="width: 33%">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="width: 34%; text-align: center"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo --><!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD><TD STYLE="width: 33%; text-align: right">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">On the fintech front, look
for iQSTEL to execute a global product launch by the end of this month to include an announcement of the MAXMO contest winners.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">On behalf of all here working
at iQSTEL, we are grateful to our shareholders for their continued confidence and support as we continue steadfastly on our planned path
for 2022 with any fanfare for our continued successes being otherwise upstaged by world events.&nbsp; Your loyalty is more valuable than
ever, and we are committed to rewarding your loyalty.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">We have initiated the Nasdaq
application process engaging the Nasdaq compliance department.&nbsp; We will keep you up to date every step of the way. The process will
take several weeks.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">We will also continue to keep
you up to date on our continued operational performance.&nbsp; Soon you will see our 2021 annual report on Form 10k. I remain confident
that our continued march toward Nasdaq, ongoing operational progress toward our $90 million 2022 revenue forecast, and the upcoming filling
or our audited 2021 financial performance will support an organic increase in our share price bringing us in compliance with our Nasdaq
uplisting objective.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Finally, look for another
management interview coming soon to hear even more details on our overall progress.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Until then, Sincerely,</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><I>Leandro Iglesias</I><BR>
CEO</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">iQSTEL Inc. (OTCQX: IQST)
(<U>www.iQSTEL.com</U>) is a US-based publicly-listed company holding an Independent Board of Directors and Independent Audit Committee
offering leading-edge services through its two business divisions and each of them with independent brands. The B2B division, Brand IQSTelecom
offering Telecommunications, Internet of Things, Technology and Blockchain platforms services, the target market for the B2B division
is Global Markets. The B2C division, Brand EVOSS offering EV Electric Motorcycles, Fintech Ecosystem, the target market for this business
division is Latin America, and the Spanish speakers in the USA. The company has presence in 15 countries, and its products and services
are used in several industries as Telecommunications, Electric Vehicle (EV), Financial Services, Chemical and Liquid Fuel Distribution
Industries. IQSTEL announced on February 17th 2021 that it became a Debt Free Company and is now completely debt free with no Convertible
Notes, Warrants, Promissory Notes or Settlement Agreements from its Balance Sheet.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 13pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><B>IQST &ndash; iQSTEL Announces
3 Target Acquisitions Expected To Close Next Month</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 13pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">New York, NY, March 24, 2022
(GLOBE NEWSWIRE) -- iQSTEL, Inc. (OTCQX: IQST) today announced the company expects to close three acquisitions prior to the end of April
2022.&nbsp; CEO Leandro Iglesias has issued a update today as part of his regular series of updates detailing the company&rsquo;s ongoing
progress toward its $90 million 2022 annual revenue forecast and uplisting to Nasdaq in the first half of this year. The update is included
in its entirety below:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Dear Shareholders:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">The first fiscal quarter of
2022 is drawing to a conclusion and in spite of the prevailing market conditions and world events, I am pleased to share that iQSTEL is
well on track to achieve its 2022 objectives.&nbsp; Nothing is standing in the way of our $90 million 2022 annual revenue forecast or
Nasdaq uplisting.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Permit me to share some highlights.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Our new electric vehicle program
is really gaining traction.&nbsp; Our dealer evaluation program is underway and our EVOSS EV Motorcycle is winning hearts and minds.&nbsp;
The feedback on the bike&rsquo;s look and feel and performance is all positive.&nbsp; Dealers are responding enthusiastically overall.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Our opportunity for the EVOSS
EV Motorcycle is already growing beyond Latin America.&nbsp; We had a dealer from Nigeria come to evaluate the EVOSS EV Motorcycle in
Miami.&nbsp; The interest was high.&nbsp; Nigeria is a country with more than 200 million people and is an overall good fit for our EVOSS
EV Motorcycle.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">On the Fintech front, I am
proud to announce the launch of our MAXMO product.&nbsp; MAXMO is the first product in our coming line of Global Money One products. Learn
more about MAXMO from our digital brochure in our Global Money One Official Channel on YouTube:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><U>https://bit.ly/IQST-MAXMO</U></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">We are in the home stretch
of developing an instrumental partnership in Latin America for our MAXMO product that alone might guarantee we reach our 2022 end user
and revenue forecast for our Fintech business line.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Our Fintech product line is
one of iQSTEL&rsquo;s primary strategies over the next 5 years expected to capture over $100 million in revenue with an estimated 30%
profit margin.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">I have mentioned before that
our M&amp;A efforts are ongoing, and they have continued with little fanfare until today.&nbsp; Now, I am pleased to announce that we
expect to finalize and close three acquisitions prior to April 30, 2022.&nbsp; Look for more details as the closing date approaches.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">iQSTEL Inc. (OTCQX: IQST)
(<U>www.iQSTEL.com</U>) is a US-based publicly-listed company holding an Independent Board of Directors and Independent Audit Committee
offering leading-edge services through its two business divisions and each of them with independent brands. The B2B division, Brand IQSTelecom
offering Telecommunications, Internet of Things, Technology and Blockchain platforms services, the target market for the B2B division
is Global Markets. The B2C division, Brand EVOSS offering EV Electric Motorcycles, Fintech Ecosystem, the target market for this business
division is Latin America, and the Spanish speakers in the USA. The company has presence in 15 countries, and its products and services
are used in several industries as Telecommunications, Electric Vehicle (EV), Financial Services, Chemical and Liquid Fuel Distribution
Industries. IQSTEL announced on February 17th 2021 that it became a Debt Free Company and is now completely debt free with no Convertible
Notes, Warrants, Promissory Notes or Settlement Agreements from its Balance Sheet.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 21.5pt/107% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0pt; background-color: white; color: #444444"><B>IQST - iQSTEL
Anticipates April Inflection Point</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 21.5pt/107% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0pt; background-color: white; color: #444444"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0pt; background-color: white; color: #444444">NEW YORK,&nbsp;March 31,
2022&nbsp;/PRNewswire/ -- iQSTEL, Inc. (OTCQX: IQST) today announced a new agreement that substantially expands the company's fintech
service offering reach. CEO&nbsp;Leandro Iglesias&nbsp;characterizes the agreement as the beginning of what he anticipates as an overall
inflection point for iQSTEL in his shareholder update included in its entirety below:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0pt; background-color: white; color: #444444">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/18pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #444444"><IMG SRC="image_001.jpg" ALT="https:||mma.prnewswire.com|media|1777493|iQSTEL_Tarjeta_Leandro.jpg" STYLE="height: 230px; width: 400px"></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Dear shareholders:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">I see April as a very big
month for iQSTEL as we continue on track toward our&nbsp;$90 million&nbsp;annual revenue forecast and Nasdaq uplisting within the first
six months of this year.&nbsp; Soon, our audited financial report will be published for 2021 verifying our monumental financial performance
last year and offering further credibility to our forecast for this year. Our Q1 2022 results will not be far behind further bolstering
confidence in our 2022 forecast.&nbsp; To kick-off what I believe will be an inflection point for the company in April, I'm pleased to
announce a new agreement that substantially expands the reach of our fintech services.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">iQSTEL, through our Global
Money One subsidiary, has entered into a partnership agreement with COOITZA RL, one of the largest and most innovative cooperatives in&nbsp;Guatemala.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">iQSTEL will be backing COOITZA
RL with our Global Money One fintech technology solution that founded our MAXMO (<U>www.maxmo.vip</U>) service offering to create for
COOITZ RL their own MAXMO-like branded offering.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">MAXMO Digital Brochure in
English:&nbsp;<U>https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=SeBxQeFpV1M&amp;t=6s</U></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">MAXMO Digital Brochure in
Spanish:&nbsp;<U>https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mc8bZr7qxAU</U>&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><TD STYLE="width: 33%">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="width: 34%; text-align: center"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo --><!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD><TD STYLE="width: 33%; text-align: right">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Cooperatives are common financial
services organizations in&nbsp;Central America&nbsp;comparable to Credit Union organizations in&nbsp;North America. COOITZA RL is an autonomous
association of individuals united voluntarily to meet their common economic, social, and cultural needs and aspirations through a jointly
owned enterprise where board members are democratically elected by the COOITZA RL individual members.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Specifically, COOITZA RL
provides its members with financing to acquire homes, working capital for their businesses, savings accounts, and micro-loans not typically
offered by banks in&nbsp;Central America.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">COOITZA RL's services extend
beyond the Guatemalan&nbsp;borders. Through the partnership agreement with COOITZA RL, we anticipate servicing 20,000 member cardholders
in the&nbsp;USA&nbsp;within the first year of launching. The COOITZA RL partnership alone has the potential to meet iQSTEL's entire fintech
services forecast for 2022.&nbsp; COOITZA RL and iQSTEL plan to launch a co-branded fintech service offering by&nbsp;April 30, 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">I think the COOITZA RL partnership
will ignite an April inflection for iQSTEL further fueled by our soon to be published audited financial results for 2021 and our ongoing
Nasdaq uplisting progress.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">We do plan to file an extension
in order to thoroughly review what we believe are landmark results. We expect to publish the 2021 annual financial report within the extension
period. I believe you will consider the extra few days worth the wait, when you review the report.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">In response to our ongoing
Nasdaq application process, our latest efforts are focused on the creation of code of conduct and ethics required by Nasdaq. We expect
to have this completed and published shortly.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">On behalf of all iQSTEL management,
employees and board members, I want to extend my thanks to all shareholders for your confidence in our journey over the last few years
that has brought us to what I expect to be a history making year for&nbsp;our&nbsp;company.&nbsp; In that history, I believe&nbsp;April
2022&nbsp;will be seen as the inflection point where our share price not only began to connect with our past performance, but also to
reflect our achievable future.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Sincerely,<BR>
<I>Leandro Iglesias</I><BR>
CEO</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">iQSTEL Inc. (OTCQX: IQST)

<P STYLE="font: 13pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><B>IQST &ndash; iQSTEL Announces
37% Revenue Growth In Q1 To $19.3 Million Based On Preliminary Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 13pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">New York, NY, April 07, 2022
(GLOBE NEWSWIRE) -- iQSTEL, Inc. (OTCQX: IQST) today announced preliminary results for the first quarter of 2022 with estimated revenue
reaching $19.3 million. This is a 37% increase over the $14.2 million reported in for the same period the previous year. &nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">The company expects to imminently
publish the audited financial report for 2021 verifying exceptional year of year growth and improving profitability.&nbsp; The 2021 audited
financial report is expected to be one of the essential last steps towards the company&rsquo;s Nasdaq uplisting objective.&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">See CEO Leandro Iglesias latest
shareholder letter update reporting on the company&rsquo;s progress in advancing on its Nasdaq uplisting objective and 2022 $90 million
revenue forecast.&nbsp; The letter is included in its entirety below:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Dear Shareholders:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">iQSTEL continues to thrive
in 2022.&nbsp; Pending the final release of our audited financial results for FY-2021, I am pleased to share with you the company&rsquo;s
preliminary results for Q1 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">The preliminary revenue for
Q1 2022 is $19.3 million.&nbsp; That is a 9.5% increase over the $17.8 million in estimated revenue reported in Q4 2021 and a 37% increase
over the revenue reported in Q1-2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">iQSTEL is well on track to
reach or surpass our $90 million 2022 revenue forecast.&nbsp; Historically, iQSTEL&rsquo;s revenue in the second half of the year is always
higher than in the first half of the year. This historical pattern provides further confidence in our trajectory toward the $90 million
2022 revenue forecast.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">We continue to improve operational
efficiencies to affect profit improvements.&nbsp; Our ongoing cost reductions in our Telecom Division achieved by taking advantage of
operational synergies are not only improving profitability but resulting in service delivery improvements and increased customer satisfaction.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt">We
intend to publish our FY 2021 audited financial results next week prior to March 15</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-size: 9pt"><SUP>th</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt">,
the amended due date after the company filed an extension last week. iQSTEL&rsquo;s Independent Audit Committee will review the results
prior to release and our Independent Board of Directors will approve the results prior to release.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt"></FONT></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><TD STYLE="width: 33%">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="width: 34%; text-align: center"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo --><!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD><TD STYLE="width: 33%; text-align: right">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">I remain confident in my statement
last week that I expect April to be an inflection point for iQSTEL.&nbsp; I encourage readers here to review&nbsp;<U>my shareholder letter
form last week</U>.&nbsp; I anticipate the publication of iQSTEL&rsquo;s audited financial report for FY 2021 to validate the company&rsquo;s
growth curve and unlock market awareness that in turn brings institutional investment interest supporting an organic increase in share
price that can bring iQSTEL in line with the minimum Nasdaq listing requirement.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Thank you for your ongoing
interest in iQSTEL and your support.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">Sincerely,<BR>
<I>Leandro Iglesias</I><BR>
CEO</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/18pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white; color: #444444">iQSTEL Inc. (OTCQX: IQST)
(<U>www.iQSTEL.com</U>) is a US-based publicly-listed company holding an Independent Board of Directors and Independent Audit Committee
offering leading-edge services through its two business divisions and each of them with independent brands. The B2B division, Brand IQSTelecom
offering Telecommunications, Internet of Things, Technology and Blockchain platforms services, the target market for the B2B division
is Global Markets. The B2C division, Brand EVOSS offering EV Electric Motorcycles, Fintech Ecosystem, the target market for this business
division is Latin America, and the Spanish speakers in the USA. The company has presence in 15 countries, and its products and services
are used in several industries as Telecommunications, Electric Vehicle (EV), Financial Services, Chemical and Liquid Fuel Distribution
Industries. IQSTEL announced on February 17th 2021 that it became a Debt Free Company and is now completely debt free with no Convertible
Notes, Warrants, Promissory Notes or Settlement Agreements from its Balance Sheet.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; color: #222222"><B></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; color: #222222"><B>IQST &ndash; iQSTEL Announces 44% Year Over Year
Revenue Growth To $64.7 Million With 59% Gross Profit Increase </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; color: #222222"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; color: #222222">New York, NY &ndash; April 18, 2022 - iQSTEL, Inc.
(OTCQX: IQST) today announced the company has published its 2021 annual report with an audited financial statement on SEC Form 10K. In
2021, iQSTEL realized a 44% increase in revenue over 2020 reaching $64.7 million compared $44.9 million the year prior. The company also
realized a year over year 59% increase in gross profit.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; color: #222222">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; color: #222222">CEO Leandro Iglesias has published a shareholder letter
included in its entirety below to address the higlights of the 2021 annual report. Mr. Iglesias plans to publish a second letter on Thursday,
April 21, 2022 to provide shareholders with the latest updates on iQSTEL&rsquo;s continuing progress toward its 2022 objectives in light
of the momentum the company achieved in 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">Dear Shareholders:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">On behalf of everyone working at iQSTEL to dilligently advance the
company, I&rsquo;m proud to highlight here the exceptional results of their dedicated efforts. I believe the 2021 audited financial results
are a meaningful indication of the company&rsquo;s potential to achieve our stated 2022 objectives. Today, will focus on the 2021 results
and in a follow up letter later this week, I will address how I feel these results substantiate our potential to achieve our 2022 objectives.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">iQSTEL&rsquo;s 2021 revenue increased 44% year over year to $64.7 million,
and the gross profit increased 59%. Increasing revenues and improving gross margins contributed to a substantial bottom line improvement
with the company&rsquo;s consolidated net loss decreasing 42% year over year. The company&rsquo;s balance sheet also improved dramatically
resulting in an overall 368% increase in shareholder equity.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">Below I have included a chart summarizing the year over year operating
performance and balance sheet improvements.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/150% Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="color: #1D2228; background-color: white">iQSTEL Inc. (OTCQX:
IQST) (</FONT><FONT STYLE="color: #188FFF; background-color: white">www.iQSTEL.com</FONT><FONT STYLE="color: #1D2228; background-color: white">)
is a US-based publicly-listed company holding an Independent Board of Directors and Independent Audit Committee offering leading-edge
services through its two business divisions and each of them with independent brands. The B2B division, Brand IQSTelecom offering Telecommunications,
Internet of Things, Technology and Blockchain platforms services, the target market for the B2B division is Global Markets. The B2C division,
Brand EVOSS offering EV Electric Motorcycles, Fintech Ecosystem, the target market for this business division is Latin America, and the
Spanish speakers in the USA. The company has presence in 15 countries, and its products and services are used in several industries as
Telecommunications, Electric Vehicle (EV), Financial Services, Chemical and Liquid Fuel Distribution Industries. IQSTEL announced on February
17th 2021 that it became a Debt Free Company and is now completely debt free with no Convertible Notes, Warrants, Promissory Notes or
Settlement Agreements from its Balance Sheet. </FONT></P>
